        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            function isInViewport(element) {
                const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
                return (
                    rect.top >= 0 &&
                    rect.left >= 0 &&
                    rect.bottom <= (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight) &&
                    rect.right <= (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth)
                );
            }

            function isPartiallyInViewport(element) {
                const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
                return (
                    rect.top >= 0 &&
                    rect.left >= 0 &&
                    rect.top <= (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight) &&
                    rect.right <= (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth)
                );
            }

            let shouldSkip = false;
            document.querySelectorAll('section').forEach(function(section) {
                if (shouldSkip) return;
                if (isInViewport(section)) {
                    section.querySelectorAll('img').forEach(function(i) {
                        i.removeAttribute('loading');
                    })
                } else if (isPartiallyInViewport(section)) {
                    section.querySelectorAll('img').forEach(function(i) {
                        if (isPartiallyInViewport(i)) {
                            i.removeAttribute('loading');
                        }
                    });
                    shouldSkip = true;
                } else {
                    shouldSkip = true;
                }
            });
        });

                                }

                            }
                        }

                            break;
                        }
                        element = element.parentElement;
                    }
                }

        var xhr;
        var discussion_ids = {"discussion_ids": []};
        const isMobile = () => window.matchMedia("(max-width: 481px)").matches;

        var updateCommentCount = function(discussion_ids){
            if(!xhr && discussion_ids.discussion_ids !== undefined && discussion_ids.discussion_ids.length !=0){
                xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                xhr.open("POST", "https://ctnozXry4dq7.engagently.com/counts/commentaries/nozXry4dq7/batch");
                xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
                xhr.onload = function () {
                    if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
                        var counts = [];
                        try{
                            counts = JSON.parse(xhr.response);
                        } catch (error) {}
                        for(const [key, value] of Object.entries(counts)){
                            let counters = document.querySelectorAll("[comment-counter-id='" + key + "']");
                            try{
                                if(counters.length > 0){
                                    if(value !== undefined && value > 0){
                                        counters.forEach(function (el) {
                                            let span = document.createElement("span");
                                            span.className = 'commentaries';
                                            if(value === 1){
                                                span.innerHTML = "1 Leserkommentar";
                                            } else {
                                                span.innerHTML = value + " Leserkommentare";
                                            }
                                            let content;
                                            if(el.getAttribute("link") !== null && el.getAttribute("link").trim() !== "" && (!isMobile() || el.getAttribute("metabox" || "").trim() === "metabox")){
                                                let a = document.createElement("a");
                                                //
                                                a.setAttribute("href", el.getAttribute("link"));
                                                a.setAttribute("target", el.getAttribute("target"));
                                                //
                                                a.setAttribute("class", el.getAttribute("linkClasses"));
                                                a.setAttribute("title", el.getAttribute("title"));
                                                content = a;
                                            }

                                            if(content !== undefined){
                                                content.appendChild(span);
                                            } else {
                                                content = span;
                                            }

                                            if(el.replaceWith && content){
                                                el.replaceWith(content);
                                            }
                                        });
                                    } else {
                                        counters.forEach(function (el) {
                                            if(el.remove){
                                                el.remove();
                                            }
                                        });
                                    }
                                }
                            } catch (error) {}
                            let previews =  document.querySelectorAll("[comment-count-preview-id='" + key + "']");
                            try{
                                if(previews.length > 0){
                                    if(value !== undefined && value > 0){
                                        previews.forEach(function (el) {
                                            if(value === 0){
                                                el.innerHTML = "Noch keine Leserkommentare";
                                            }else if(value === 1){
                                                el.innerHTML = "1 Leserkommentar";
                                            }else {
                                                el.innerHTML = value + " Leserkommentare";
                                            }
                                        });
                                    }
                                }
                            } catch (error) {}
                        }
                        for(const el of document.querySelectorAll("[class='comment-counter']")){
                            if(el.remove){
                                el.remove();
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    xhr = null;
                };
                xhr.send(JSON.stringify(discussion_ids));
            }
        };

        var findDiscussions = function(){
            var newcounterids = [];
            document.querySelectorAll("[class='comment-counter']").forEach(function(n){
                var id =n.getAttribute('comment-counter-id');
                if(!discussion_ids.discussion_ids.includes(id)){
                    newcounterids.push(id);
                }
            });
            return newcounterids;
        };

        function do_tcf_engagently_count() {
            const initCount = () => {
                discussion_ids.discussion_ids = findDiscussions();
                updateCommentCount(discussion_ids);

                const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
                    discussion_ids.discussion_ids = findDiscussions();
                    updateCommentCount(discussion_ids);
                });

                observer.observe(document.documentElement, {
                    childList: true,
                    subtree: true
                });
            };

            if (document.readyState === "loading") {
                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", init);
            } else {
                initCount();
            }
        }

      (function () {
        function injectConsentListener() {
          if (typeof window.__tcfapi !== "function") {
            // Warten bis __tcfapi verfügbar ist
            setTimeout(injectConsentListener, 100);
            return;
          }

          window.__tcfapi("addEventListener", 2, (tcData, success) => {
            console.log("tcf Event listener injected");
            if (success && (tcData.eventStatus === "tcloaded" || tcData.eventStatus === "useractioncomplete")) {
              window.__tcfapi("getCustomVendorConsents", 2, (data, ok) => {
                check_all_tcf_consents(data);
              });
            }
          });
        }

        // Wenn das DOM geladen ist, starte den Injection-Prozess
        if (document.readyState === "complete" || document.readyState === "interactive") {
          injectConsentListener();
        } else {
          document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", injectConsentListener);
        }
      })();
    </script><!-- end gtm --><script>
        // Script Load Function

        function load_tcf_script(src, cb, engagently = false, targetId = false, id = false) {
            if (document.querySelector(`script[src="${src}"]`)) {
                cb && cb(); // trotzdem Callback aufrufen, falls schon da
                return;
            }

            const s = document.createElement("script");
            s.src = src;

            if(engagently){
                s.type = "module";
                s.setAttribute("data-engagently", "initEngagently");
            }else{
                s.async = true;
            }

            if(id != false){
                s.id = id;
            }

            s.onload = s.onerror = () => cb && cb();

            if(targetId != false){
                const container = document.getElementById(targetId);
                if (!container) {
                    console.error("Container doesnt exist:", targetId);
                    return;
                }
                container.appendChild(s);
            }else{
                document.head.appendChild(s);
            }
        }

    // Load GTM
    function do_tcf_gtm(){
      console.log("consented gtm");
      (function (w, d, s, l, i) {
        w[l] = w[l] || [];
        w[l].push({ "gtm.start": new Date().getTime(), event: "gtm.js" });
        var f = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0],
            j = d.createElement(s),
            dl = l != "dataLayer" ? "&l=" + l : "";
        j.async = true;
        j.src = "https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtm.js?id=" + i + dl;
        f.parentNode.insertBefore(j, f);
      })(window, document, "script", "dataLayer", "GTM-T9XP5VJ6");
      console.log("gtm completed");
    }

        function do_tcf_temp_helper(){

        function do_tcf_engagently_check(){
            do_tcf_engagently_count();
            safeCall("do_tcf_engagently");
        }

        function do_tcf_transmatico_check(){
            document
              .querySelectorAll("script[id^='transmatico-loader-']")
              .forEach(script => {
                const id = script.id.replace("transmatico-loader-", "");
                const fnName = "do_tcf_transmatico" + id;

                if (typeof window[fnName] === "function") {
                  window[fnName]();
                } else {
                  console.warn(`Funktion ${fnName} nicht gefunden`);
                }
              });
          }

        function do_tcf_crossplan_check(){
            safeCall("do_tcf_crossplan");
        }
        function do_tcf_outbrain_check(){
            safeCall("do_tcf_outbrain");
        }

        function do_tcf_echobox_check(){
            safeCall("do_tcf_echobox");
        }

        function safeCall(fnName) {
            const fn = window[fnName];
             if (typeof fn === 'function') {
                 fn();
             }
        }

        function check_all_tcf_consents(data) {
            console.log("######consent");
            const vendorActions = {
                "5e952f6107d9d20c88e7c975": do_tcf_temp_helper,        // do_tcf_gtm Google Tag Manager
                "5e98e7f1b8e05c48537f6114": do_tcf_addefend,   // AdDefend GmbH
                "60a78129a228630f9645e6e5": do_tcf_confiant,   // Confiant Inc.  --ID vom Dienstleister nicht in der Liste
                "60e5add90015ea244706ce6a": do_tcf_crossplan_check,  // Crossplan Deutschland GmbH & Co. KG
                "5e37fc3e56a5e60dff4e1992": do_tcf_nativendo,  // Nativendo / Seeding Alliance GmbH
                "6447e86d25ed3c0654e55c37": do_tcf_transmatico_check,    // Smartico / Transsmartico
                "68ca6f8f3928976ef7e9dca2": () => {},          // Weekli (noch offen)
                "5e7ced57b8e05c485246ccde": do_tcf_outbrain_check, // Outbrain
                "6582d35f8b5d7905669500e5": do_tcf_engagently_check, // engagently (ferret go GmbH)
                "5f32c9169bbaec159efcc96c": do_tcf_echobox_check, // echobox
            };
            vendorActions['6582d35f8b5d7905669500e5'](); // Engagently immer ausführen
            Object.keys(vendorActions).forEach(vendorid => {
                const consented = data.consentedVendors?.some(v => v._id === vendorid);
                const granted   = data.grants?.[vendorid]?.vendorGrant === true;

                if (consented || granted) {
                    vendorActions[vendorid]();
                }
            });
        }

                        Versuchter heimtückischer Mord: Urteil nach Angriff auf Nachbarn in Emden
                    </h3><div class="article__teaser__intro text-color__comet">Im Prozess gegen einen 30-Jährigen aus Emden fiel jetzt vor dem Landgericht Aurich das Urteil. Der Angeklagte hatten seinen Nachbarn schwer verletzt. <script>
    function closeStickyFooterAd() {
        const stickyFooterAd = top.document.querySelector('[data="push-sticky-footer-ad"]');
        if (stickyFooterAd !== null) {
            // Fügt die Animation hinzu
            stickyFooterAd.style.transform = 'translateY(100px)';
            stickyFooterAd.style.opacity = '0';

            // Sobald die Animation abgeschlossen ist, entferne das Element
            setTimeout(() => {
                stickyFooterAd.remove();
            }, 500);
        }
    }

    const stickyFooterPush = top.document.querySelector('[data="push-sticky-footer-ad"]');
    // Intersection Observer: Ist das stickyFooterElement sichtbar, dann wird stickyFooterPush ausgeblendet
    const stickyFooterObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        let intersecting = entries[0].isIntersecting;
        if (intersecting === true) {
            stickyFooterPush.style.display = 'none';
        } else if (intersecting === false) {
            stickyFooterPush.style.removeProperty('display');
        }
    })

    const stickyFooterElement = top.document.querySelector('#default-footer');
    stickyFooterObserver.observe(stickyFooterElement);
    console.log("adframeworkfiles vorhanden");
</script>
